          <h1 id="page-title" class="page__title" itemprop="headline">
            <a href="https://gityeop.github.io/math-for-ml/statistics/" itemprop="url">통계학 맛보기
</a>
          </h1>
          

  <p class="page__meta">
    

    

    
      
      

      <span class="page__meta-readtime">
        <i class="far fa-clock" aria-hidden="true"></i>
        
          6 분 소요
        
      </span>
    
  </p>


        </header>
      

      <section class="page__content" itemprop="text">
        
        <h2 id="모수">모수<a class="header-link" href="#모수" title="Permalink"><span class="sr-only">Permalink</span><i class="fas fa-link"></i></a></h2>

<ul>
  <li>모수 : 특정 집단 전체의 특성을 나타내는 수치
    <ul>
      <li>모집단의 평균, 분산, 비율 등의 형태로 나타남</li>
    </ul>
  </li>
  <li>통계적 모델링은 적절한 가정 위에서 확률분포를 추정(inference)하는 것이 목표</li>
  <li>기계학습과 통계학이 공통적으로 추구하는 목표</li>
  <li>유한한 개수의 데이터만 관찰해서 모집단의 분포를 정확하게 알아낸 다는 것은 불가능</li>
  <li>근사적으로 확률분포를 추정할 수 밖에 없음
    <ul>
      <li>분포를 정확하게 맞춤 X</li>
      <li>데이터와 추정 방법의 불확실성을 고려</li>
    </ul>
  </li>
  <li>데이터가 <strong>특정 확률분포를 따른다고 선험적으로(a priori) 가정</strong>한 후 그 분포를 결정하는 모수(parameter)를 추정하는 방법은 <strong>모수적(parametric) 방법론</strong>이라고 함</li>
  <li>특정 <strong>확률분포를 가정하지 않고</strong> 데이터에 따라 모델의 구조 및 모수의 개수가 유연하게 바뀌면 <strong>비모수(nonparametric) 방법론</strong>이라고 함</li>
</ul>

<h2 id="확률분포-가정하기-예제">확률분포 가정하기: 예제<a class="header-link" href="#확률분포-가정하기-예제" title="Permalink"><span class="sr-only">Permalink</span><i class="fas fa-link"></i></a></h2>

<ul>
  <li>확률분포를 가정하는 방법 : 우선 히스토그램을 통해 모양을 관찰한다.</li>
  <li>데이터가 2개의 값(0 또는 1)만 가지는 경우 -&gt; 베르누이 분포</li>
  <li>데이터가 n개의 이산적인 값을 가지는 경우 -&gt; 카테고리 분포</li>
  <li>
    <p>데이터가 [0, 1] 사이에서 값을 가지는 경우 -&gt; 베타분포</p>

  </li>
  <li>데이터가 0 이상의 값을 가지는 경우 -&gt; 감마분포, 로그정규분포 등</li>
  <li>데이터가 R 전체에서 값을 가지는 경우 -&gt; 정규분포, 라플라스 분포</li>
  <li>기계적으로 확률분포를 가정해서는 안됨</li>
  <li><strong>데이터를 생성하는 원리를 먼저 고려</strong>하는 것이 원칙</li>
</ul>

<h2 id="데이터로-모수를-추정해보자">데이터로 모수를 추정해보자<a class="header-link" href="#데이터로-모수를-추정해보자" title="Permalink"><span class="sr-only">Permalink</span><i class="fas fa-link"></i></a></h2>

<ul>
  <li>데이터의 확률분포를 가정했다면 모수를 추정해볼 수 있습니다</li>
  <li>정규분포의 모수는 평균 <mjx-container class="MathJax CtxtMenu_Attached_0" jax="CHTML" tabindex="0" ctxtmenu_counter="1" style="font-size: 119%; position: relative;"><mjx-math class="MJX-TEX" aria-hidden="true"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D707 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-math><mjx-assistive-mml unselectable="on" display="inline"><mjx-container class="MathJax CtxtMenu_Attached_0" jax="CHTML" tabindex="0" ctxtmenu_counter="1" style="font-size: 118.6%; position: relative;"><mjx-math class="MJX-TEX" aria-hidden="true"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D707 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-math><mjx-assistive-mml unselectable="on" display="inline"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mi>μ</mi></math></mjx-assistive-mml></mjx-container></mjx-assistive-mml></mjx-container> 과 분산 <mjx-container class="MathJax CtxtMenu_Attached_0" jax="CHTML" tabindex="0" ctxtmenu_counter="2" style="font-size: 119%; position: relative;"><mjx-math class="MJX-TEX" aria-hidden="true"><mjx-msup><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D70E TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-script style="vertical-align: 0.363em;"><mjx-mn class="mjx-n" size="s"><mjx-c class="mjx-c32"></mjx-c></mjx-mn></mjx-script></mjx-msup></mjx-math><mjx-assistive-mml unselectable="on" display="inline"><mjx-container class="MathJax CtxtMenu_Attached_0" jax="CHTML" tabindex="0" ctxtmenu_counter="2" style="font-size: 118.6%; position: relative;"><mjx-math class="MJX-TEX" aria-hidden="true"><mjx-msup><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D70E TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-script style="vertical-align: 0.363em;"><mjx-mn class="mjx-n" size="s"><mjx-c class="mjx-c32"></mjx-c></mjx-mn></mjx-script></mjx-msup></mjx-math><mjx-assistive-mml unselectable="on" display="inline"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><msup><mi>σ</mi><mn>2</mn></msup></math></mjx-assistive-mml></mjx-container></mjx-assistive-mml></mjx-container>으로 추정하는 통계량(statistic)은 다음과 같다

<ul>
  <li>표본분산을 구할 때 <mjx-container class="MathJax CtxtMenu_Attached_0" jax="CHTML" tabindex="0" ctxtmenu_counter="7" style="font-size: 119%; position: relative;"><mjx-math class="MJX-TEX" aria-hidden="true"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D441 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-math><mjx-assistive-mml unselectable="on" display="inline"><mjx-container class="MathJax CtxtMenu_Attached_0" jax="CHTML" tabindex="0" ctxtmenu_counter="7" style="font-size: 118.6%; position: relative;"><mjx-math class="MJX-TEX" aria-hidden="true"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D441 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-math><mjx-assistive-mml unselectable="on" display="inline"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mi>N</mi></math></mjx-assistive-mml></mjx-container></mjx-assistive-mml></mjx-container>이 아니라 <mjx-container class="MathJax CtxtMenu_Attached_0" jax="CHTML" tabindex="0" ctxtmenu_counter="8" style="font-size: 119%; position: relative;"><mjx-math class="MJX-TEX" aria-hidden="true"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D441 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="3"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2212"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mn class="mjx-n" space="3"><mjx-c class="mjx-c31"></mjx-c></mjx-mn></mjx-math><mjx-assistive-mml unselectable="on" display="inline"><mjx-container class="MathJax CtxtMenu_Attached_0" jax="CHTML" tabindex="0" ctxtmenu_counter="8" style="font-size: 118.6%; position: relative;"><mjx-math class="MJX-TEX" aria-hidden="true"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D441 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="3"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2212"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mn class="mjx-n" space="3"><mjx-c class="mjx-c31"></mjx-c></mjx-mn></mjx-math><mjx-assistive-mml unselectable="on" display="inline"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mi>N</mi><mo>−</mo><mn>1</mn></math></mjx-assistive-mml></mjx-container></mjx-assistive-mml></mjx-container>로 나누는 이유는 불편(unbiased) 추정량을 구하기 위해서다</li>
  <li>통계량의 확률분포를 표집분포(sampling distribution)라 부르며, 특히 표본평균의 표집분포는 <mjx-container class="MathJax CtxtMenu_Attached_0" jax="CHTML" tabindex="0" ctxtmenu_counter="9" style="font-size: 119%; position: relative;"><mjx-math class="MJX-TEX" aria-hidden="true"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D441 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-math><mjx-assistive-mml unselectable="on" display="inline"><mjx-container class="MathJax CtxtMenu_Attached_0" jax="CHTML" tabindex="0" ctxtmenu_counter="9" style="font-size: 118.6%; position: relative;"><mjx-math class="MJX-TEX" aria-hidden="true"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D441 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-math><mjx-assistive-mml unselectable="on" display="inline"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mi>N</mi></math></mjx-assistive-mml></mjx-container></mjx-assistive-mml></mjx-container>이 커질수록 정규분포 <mjx-container class="MathJax CtxtMenu_Attached_0" jax="CHTML" tabindex="0" ctxtmenu_counter="10" style="font-size: 119%; position: relative;"><mjx-math class="MJX-TEX" aria-hidden="true"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D441 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c28"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D707 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2C"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-msup space="2"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D70E TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-script style="vertical-align: 0.363em;"><mjx-mn class="mjx-n" size="s"><mjx-c class="mjx-c32"></mjx-c></mjx-mn></mjx-script></mjx-msup><mjx-texatom texclass="ORD"><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2F"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-texatom><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D441 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c29"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-math><mjx-assistive-mml unselectable="on" display="inline"><mjx-container class="MathJax CtxtMenu_Attached_0" jax="CHTML" tabindex="0" ctxtmenu_counter="10" style="font-size: 118.6%; position: relative;"><mjx-math class="MJX-TEX" aria-hidden="true"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D441 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c28"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D707 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2C"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-msup space="2"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D70E TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-script style="vertical-align: 0.363em;"><mjx-mn class="mjx-n" size="s"><mjx-c class="mjx-c32"></mjx-c></mjx-mn></mjx-script></mjx-msup><mjx-texatom texclass="ORD"><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2F"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-texatom><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D441 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c29"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-math><mjx-assistive-mml unselectable="on" display="inline"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mi>N</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>μ</mi><mo>,</mo><msup><mi>σ</mi><mn>2</mn></msup><mrow data-mjx-texclass="ORD"><mo>/</mo></mrow><mi>N</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></math></mjx-assistive-mml></mjx-container></mjx-assistive-mml></mjx-container>에 근접한다.</li>
</ul>

<h2 id="표본-분포-sample-distribution">표본 분포 (Sample Distribution)<a class="header-link" href="#표본-분포-sample-distribution" title="Permalink"><span class="sr-only">Permalink</span><i class="fas fa-link"></i></a></h2>

<p>표본 분포는 단순히 어떤 모집단에서 추출한 하나의 표본 데이터의 분포를 말합니다. 예를 들어, 모집단이 있는 학생들의 키에 대한 정보라면, 100명의 학생을 임의로 선택하여 그들의 키를 기록한 값들이 표본 분포를 형성하게 됩니다.</p>

<h3 id="특징">특징<a class="header-link" href="#특징" title="Permalink"><span class="sr-only">Permalink</span><i class="fas fa-link"></i></a></h3>

<ul>
  <li>표본의 크기: 표본 분포는 주어진 표본의 크기에 따라 다릅니다.</li>
  <li>특정 데이터셋: 표본 분포는 특정 표본에 대한 데이터 분포입니다.</li>
  <li>모집단의 특성을 반영: 표본이 충분히 크다면, 모집단의 특성을 어느 정도 반영할 수 있습니다.</li>
</ul>

<h2 id="표집-분포-sampling-distribution">표집 분포 (Sampling Distribution)<a class="header-link" href="#표집-분포-sampling-distribution" title="Permalink"><span class="sr-only">Permalink</span><i class="fas fa-link"></i></a></h2>

<p>표집 분포는 동일한 모집단에서 같은 크기의 표본을 여러 번 추출하여 계산된 통계량(예: 평균, 분산)의 분포를 말합니다. 즉, 표집 분포는 많은 표본들의 통계량으로 이루어진 분포입니다.</p>

<h3 id="특징-1">특징<a class="header-link" href="#특징-1" title="Permalink"><span class="sr-only">Permalink</span><i class="fas fa-link"></i></a></h3>

<ul>
  <li>반복된 추출: 동일한 크기의 표본을 여러 번 추출하여 각각의 표본에서 계산된 통계량들의 분포입니다.</li>
  <li>통계량의 분포: 표집 분포는 특정 통계량(예: 표본 평균, 표본 비율 등)의 분포입니다.</li>
  <li>중앙 극한 정리: 표본 크기가 충분히 크다면, 표집 분포는 모집단의 분포 형태와 관계없이 정규 분포에 가까워집니다.</li>
</ul>

<h2 id="최대가능도-추정법">최대가능도 추정법<a class="header-link" href="#최대가능도-추정법" title="Permalink"><span class="sr-only">Permalink</span><i class="fas fa-link"></i></a></h2>

<ul>
  <li>표본평균이나 표본분산은 중요한 통계량이지만 확률분포마다 사용하는 모수가 다르므로 적절한 통계량이 달라지게 된다</li>
  <li>이론적으로 가장 가능성이 높은 모수를 추정하는 방법 중 하나는 최대가능도 추정법(maximum likelihood estimation, MLE)

<ol>
  <li>목표 파라미터 <mjx-container class="MathJax CtxtMenu_Attached_0" jax="CHTML" tabindex="0" ctxtmenu_counter="12" style="font-size: 119%; position: relative;"><mjx-math class="MJX-TEX" aria-hidden="true"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D703 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-math><mjx-assistive-mml unselectable="on" display="inline"><mjx-container class="MathJax CtxtMenu_Attached_0" jax="CHTML" tabindex="0" ctxtmenu_counter="12" style="font-size: 118.6%; position: relative;"><mjx-math class="MJX-TEX" aria-hidden="true"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D703 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-math><mjx-assistive-mml unselectable="on" display="inline"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mi>θ</mi></math></mjx-assistive-mml></mjx-container></mjx-assistive-mml></mjx-container> 선택:
    <ul>
      <li><mjx-container class="MathJax CtxtMenu_Attached_0" jax="CHTML" tabindex="0" ctxtmenu_counter="13" style="font-size: 119%; position: relative;"><mjx-math class="MJX-TEX" aria-hidden="true"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D703 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-math><mjx-assistive-mml unselectable="on" display="inline"><mjx-container class="MathJax CtxtMenu_Attached_0" jax="CHTML" tabindex="0" ctxtmenu_counter="13" style="font-size: 118.6%; position: relative;"><mjx-math class="MJX-TEX" aria-hidden="true"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D707 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-math><mjx-assistive-mml unselectable="on" display="inline"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mi>μ</mi></math></mjx-assistive-mml></mjx-container></mjx-assistive-mml></mjx-container>와 <mjx-container class="MathJax CtxtMenu_Attached_0" jax="CHTML" tabindex="0" ctxtmenu_counter="15" style="font-size: 119%;     </ul>

  <li>데이터 <mjx-container class="MathJax CtxtMenu_Attached_0" jax="CHTML" tabindex="0" ctxtmenu_counter="16" style="font-size: 119%; position: relative;"><mjx-math class="MJX-TEX" aria-hidden="true"><mjx-texatom texclass="ORD"><mjx-mi class="mjx-b"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D431 TEX-B"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-texatom></mjx-math><mjx-assistive-mml unselectable="on" display="inline"><mjx-container class="MathJax CtxtMenu_Attached_0" jax="CHTML" tabindex="0" ctxtmenu_counter="16" style="font-size: 118.6%; position: relative;"><mjx-math class="MJX-TEX" aria-hidden="true"><mjx-texatom texclass="ORD"><mjx-mi class="mjx-b"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D431 TEX-B"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-texatom></mjx-math><mjx-assistive-mml unselectable="on" display="inline"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mrow data-mjx-texclass="ORD"><mi mathvariant="bold">x</mi></mrow></math></mjx-assistive-mml></mjx-container></mjx-assistive-mml></mjx-container>:
    <ul>
      <li><mjx-container class="MathJax CtxtMenu_Attached_0" jax="CHTML" tabindex="0" ctxtmenu_counter="17" style="font-size: 119%; position: relative;"><mjx-math class="MJX-TEX" aria-hidden="true"><mjx-texatom texclass="ORD"><mjx-mi class="mjx-b"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D431 TEX-B"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-texatom></mjx-math><mjx-assistive-mml unselectable="on" display="inline"><mjx-container class="MathJax CtxtMenu_Attached_0" jax="CHTML" tabindex="0" ctxtmenu_counter="17" style="font-size: 118.6%; position: relative;"><mjx-math class="MJX-TEX" aria-hidden="true"><mjx-texatom texclass="ORD"><mjx-mi class="mjx-b"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D431 TEX-B"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-texatom></mjx-math><mjx-assistive-mml unselectable="on" display="inline"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mrow data-mjx-texclass="ORD"><mi mathvariant="bold">x</mi></mrow></math></mjx-assistive-mml></mjx-container></mjx-assistive-mml></mjx-container>는 실제 관측된 데이터입니다. 예를 들어, 어떤 실험에서 얻은 결과나 측정값들입니다.</li>

  <li>우도 함수 <mjx-container class="MathJax CtxtMenu_Attached_0" jax="CHTML" tabindex="0" ctxtmenu_counter="18" style="font-size: 119%; position: relative;"><mjx-math class="MJX-TEX" aria-hidden="true"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D43F TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c28"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D703 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c3B"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-texatom space="2" texclass="ORD"><mjx-mi class="mjx-b"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D431 TEX-B"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-texatom><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c29"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-math><mjx-assistive-mml unselectable="on" display="inline"><mjx-container class="MathJax CtxtMenu_Attached_0" jax="CHTML" tabindex="0" ctxtmenu_counter="18" style="font-size: 118.6%; position: relative;"><mjx-math class="MJX-TEX" aria-hidden="true"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D43F TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c28"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D703 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c3B"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-texatom space="2" texclass="ORD"><mjx-mi class="mjx-b"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D431 TEX-B"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-texatom><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c29"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-math><mjx-assistive-mml unselectable="on" display="inline"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mi>L</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>θ</mi><mo>;</mo><mrow data-mjx-texclass="ORD"><mi mathvariant="bold">x</mi></mrow><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></math></mjx-assistive-mml></mjx-container></mjx-assistive-mml></mjx-container>:
    <ul>
      <li>우도 함수는 주어진 파라미터 <mjx-container class="MathJax CtxtMenu_Attached_0" jax="CHTML" tabindex="0" ctxtmenu_counter="19" style="font-size: 119%; position: relative;"><mjx-math class="MJX-TEX" aria-hidden="true"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D703 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-math><mjx-assistive-mml unselectable="on" display="inline"><mjx-container class="MathJax CtxtMenu_Attached_0" jax="CHTML" tabindex="0" ctxtmenu_counter="19" style="font-size: 118.6%; position: relative;"><mjx-math class="MJX-TEX" aria-hidden="true"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D703 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-math><mjx-assistive-mml unselectable="on" display="inline"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mi>θ</mi></math></mjx-assistive-mml></mjx-container></mjx-assistive-mml></mjx-container>에 대해 데이터 <mjx-container class="MathJax CtxtMenu_Attached_0" jax="CHTML" tabindex="0" ctxtmenu_counter="20" style="font-size: 119%; position: relative;"><mjx-math class="MJX-TEX" aria-hidden="true"><mjx-texatom texclass="ORD"><mjx-mi class="mjx-b"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D431 TEX-B"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-texatom></mjx-math><mjx-assistive-mml unselectable="on" display="inline"><mjx-container class="MathJax CtxtMenu_Attached_0" jax="CHTML" tabindex="0" ctxtmenu_counter="20" style="font-size: 118.6%; position: relative;"><mjx-math class="MJX-TEX" aria-hidden="true"><mjx-texatom texclass="ORD"><mjx-mi class="mjx-b"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D431 TEX-B"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-texatom></mjx-math><mjx-assistive-mml unselectable="on" display="inline"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mrow data-mjx-texclass="ORD"><mi mathvariant="bold">x</mi></mrow></math></mjx-assistive-mml></mjx-container></mjx-assistive-mml></mjx-container>가 관측될 확률을 나타냅니다.

      <li>여기서 <mjx-container class="MathJax CtxtMenu_Attached_0" jax="CHTML" tabindex="0" ctxtmenu_counter="22" style="font-size: 119%; position: relative;"><mjx-math class="MJX-TEX" aria-hidden="true"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D443 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c28"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-texatom texclass="ORD"><mjx-mi class="mjx-b"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D431 TEX-B"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-texatom><mjx-texatom texclass="ORD"><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c7C"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-texatom><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D703 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c29"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-math><mjx-assistive-mml unselectable="on" display="inline"><mjx-container class="MathJax CtxtMenu_Attached_0" jax="CHTML" tabindex="0" ctxtmenu_counter="22" style="font-size: 118.6%; position: relative;"><mjx-math class="MJX-TEX" aria-hidden="true"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D443 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c28"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-texatom texclass="ORD"><mjx-mi class="mjx-b"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D431 TEX-B"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-texatom><mjx-texatom texclass="ORD"><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c7C"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-texatom><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D703 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c29"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-math><mjx-assistive-mml unselectable="on" display="inline"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mi>P</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mrow data-mjx-texclass="ORD"><mi mathvariant="bold">x</mi></mrow><mrow data-mjx-texclass="ORD"><mo stretchy="false">|</mo></mrow><mi>θ</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></math></mjx-assistive-mml></mjx-container></mjx-assistive-mml></mjx-container>는 조건부 확률로,
<mjx-container class="MathJax CtxtMenu_Attached_0" jax="CHTML" tabindex="0" ctxtmenu_counter="23" style="font-size: 119%; position: relative;"><mjx-math class="MJX-TEX" aria-hidden="true"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D703 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-math><mjx-assistive-mml unselectable="on" display="inline"><mjx-container class="MathJax CtxtMenu_Attached_0" jax="CHTML" tabindex="0" ctxtmenu_counter="23" style="font-size: 118.6%; position: relative;"><mjx-math class="MJX-TEX" aria-hidden="true"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D703 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-math><mjx-assistive-mml unselectable="on" display="inline"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mi>θ</mi></math></mjx-assistive-mml></mjx-container></mjx-assistive-mml></mjx-container>가 주어졌을 때 <mjx-container class="MathJax CtxtMenu_Attached_0" jax="CHTML" tabindex="0" ctxtmenu_counter="24" style="font-size: 119%; position: relative;"><mjx-math class="MJX-TEX" aria-hidden="true"><mjx-texatom texclass="ORD"><mjx-mi class="mjx-b"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D431 TEX-B"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-texatom></mjx-math><mjx-assistive-mml unselectable="on" display="inline"><mjx-container class="MathJax CtxtMenu_Attached_0" jax="CHTML" tabindex="0" ctxtmenu_counter="24" style="font-size: 118.6%; position: relative;"><mjx-math class="MJX-TEX" aria-hidden="true"><mjx-texatom texclass="ORD"><mjx-mi class="mjx-b"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D431 TEX-B"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-texatom></mjx-math><mjx-assistive-mml unselectable="on" display="inline"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mrow data-mjx-texclass="ORD"><mi mathvariant="bold">x</mi></mrow></math></mjx-assistive-mml></mjx-container></mjx-assistive-mml></mjx-container>가 관측될 확률을 의미합니다.</li>
    </ul>
  </li>
  <li><mjx-container class="MathJax CtxtMenu_Attached_0" jax="CHTML" tabindex="0" ctxtmenu_counter="25" style="font-size: 119%; position: relative;"><mjx-math class="MJX-TEX" aria-hidden="true"><mjx-munder><mjx-row><mjx-base><mjx-mi class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c61"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c72"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c67"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c6D"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c61"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c78"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-base></mjx-row><mjx-row><mjx-under style="padding-top: 0.167em; padding-left: 1.461em;"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i" size="s"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D703 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-under></mjx-row></mjx-munder></mjx-math><mjx-assistive-mml unselectable="on" display="inline"><mjx-container class="MathJax CtxtMenu_Attached_0" jax="CHTML" tabindex="0" ctxtmenu_counter="25" style="font-size: 118.6%; position: relative;"><mjx-math class="MJX-TEX" aria-hidden="true"><mjx-munder><mjx-row><mjx-base><mjx-mi class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c61"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c72"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c67"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c6D"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c61"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c78"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-base></mjx-row><mjx-row><mjx-under style="padding-top: 0.167em; padding-left: 1.461em;"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i" size="s"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D703 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-under></mjx-row></mjx-munder></mjx-math><mjx-assistive-mml unselectable="on" display="inline"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><munder><mi>argmax</mi><mi>θ</mi></munder></math></mjx-assistive-mml></mjx-container></mjx-assistive-mml></mjx-container>:
    <ul>
      <li>이 부분은 “우도 함수 <mjx-container class="MathJax CtxtMenu_Attached_0" jax="CHTML" tabindex="0" ctxtmenu_counter="26" style="font-size: 119%; position: relative;"><mjx-math class="MJX-TEX" aria-hidden="true"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D43F TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c28"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D703 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c3B"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-texatom space="2" texclass="ORD"><mjx-mi class="mjx-b"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D431 TEX-B"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-texatom><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c29"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-math><mjx-assistive-mml unselectable="on" display="inline"><mjx-container class="MathJax CtxtMenu_Attached_0" jax="CHTML" tabindex="0" ctxtmenu_counter="26" style="font-size: 118.6%; position: relative;"><mjx-math class="MJX-TEX" aria-hidden="true"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D43F TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c28"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D703 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c3B"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-texatom space="2" texclass="ORD"><mjx-mi class="mjx-b"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D431 TEX-B"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-texatom><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c29"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-math><mjx-assistive-mml unselectable="on" display="inline"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mi>L</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>θ</mi><mo>;</mo><mrow data-mjx-texclass="ORD"><mi mathvariant="bold">x</mi></mrow><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></math></mjx-assistive-mml></mjx-container></mjx-assistive-mml></mjx-container>를 최대화하는 <mjx-container class="MathJax CtxtMenu_Attached_0" jax="CHTML" tabindex="0" ctxtmenu_counter="27" style="font-size: 119%; position: relative;"><mjx-math class="MJX-TEX" aria-hidden="true"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D703 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-math><mjx-assistive-mml unselectable="on" display="inline"><mjx-container class="MathJax CtxtMenu_Attached_0" jax="CHTML" tabindex="0" ctxtmenu_counter="27" style="font-size: 118.6%; position: relative;"><mjx-math class="MJX-TEX" aria-hidden="true"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D703 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-math><mjx-assistive-mml unselectable="on" display="inline"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mi>θ</mi></math></mjx-assistive-mml></mjx-container></mjx-assistive-mml></mjx-container>를 찾는다”는 의미입니다.</li>
      <li>즉, 가능한 모든 <mjx-container class="MathJax CtxtMenu_Attached_0" jax="CHTML" tabindex="0" ctxtmenu_counter="28" style="font-size: 119%; position: relative;"><mjx-math class="MJX-TEX" aria-hidden="true"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D703 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-math><mjx-assistive-mml unselectable="on" display="inline"><mjx-container class="MathJax CtxtMenu_Attached_0" jax="CHTML" tabindex="0" ctxtmenu_counter="28" style="font-size: 118.6%; position: relative;"><mjx-math class="MJX-TEX" aria-hidden="true"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D703 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-math><mjx-assistive-mml unselectable="on" display="inline"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mi>θ</mi></math></mjx-assistive-mml></mjx-container></mjx-assistive-mml></mjx-container> 값 중에서 데이터 <mjx-container class="MathJax CtxtMenu_Attached_0" jax="CHTML" tabindex="0" ctxtmenu_counter="29" style="font-size: 119%; position: relative;"><mjx-math class="MJX-TEX" aria-hidden="true"><mjx-texatom texclass="ORD"><mjx-mi class="mjx-b"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D431 TEX-B"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-texatom></mjx-math><mjx-assistive-mml unselectable="on" display="inline"><mjx-container class="MathJax CtxtMenu_Attached_0" jax="CHTML" tabindex="0" ctxtmenu_counter="29" style="font-size: 118.6%; position: relative;"><mjx-math class="MJX-TEX" aria-hidden="true"><mjx-texatom texclass="ORD"><mjx-mi class="mjx-b"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D431 TEX-B"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-texatom></mjx-math><mjx-assistive-mml unselectable="on" display="inline"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mrow data-mjx-texclass="ORD"><mi mathvariant="bold">x</mi></mrow></math></mjx-assistive-mml></mjx-container></mjx-assistive-mml></mjx-container>가 관측될 확률을 가장 크게 만드는 <mjx-container class="MathJax CtxtMenu_Attached_0" jax="CHTML" tabindex="0" ctxtmenu_counter="30" style="font-size: 119%; position: relative;"><mjx-math class="MJX-TEX" aria-hidden="true"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D703 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-math><mjx-assistive-mml unselectable="on" display="inline"><mjx-container class="MathJax CtxtMenu_Attached_0" jax="CHTML" tabindex="0" ctxtmenu_counter="30" style="font-size: 118.6%; position: relative;"><mjx-math class="MJX-TEX" aria-hidden="true"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D703 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-math><mjx-assistive-mml unselectable="on" display="inline"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mi>θ</mi></math></mjx-assistive-mml></mjx-container></mjx-assistive-mml></mjx-container>를 찾는 과정입니다.</li>
    </ul>
  </li>
  <li>최대우도추정 <mjx-container class="MathJax CtxtMenu_Attached_0" jax="CHTML" tabindex="0" ctxtmenu_counter="31" style="font-size: 119%; position: relative;"><mjx-math class="MJX-TEX" aria-hidden="true"><mjx-msub><mjx-texatom texclass="ORD"><mjx-mover><mjx-over style="padding-bottom: 0.105em;     <ul>
      <li>위 과정을 통해 찾은 <mjx-container class="MathJax CtxtMenu_Attached_0" jax="CHTML" tabindex="0" ctxtmenu_counter="32" style="font-size: 119%; position: relative;"><mjx-math class="MJX-TEX" aria-hidden="true"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D703 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-math><mjx-assistive-mml unselectable="on" display="inline"><mjx-container class="MathJax CtxtMenu_Attached_0" jax="CHTML" tabindex="0" ctxtmenu_counter="32" style="font-size: 118.6%;       <li><mjx-container class="MathJax CtxtMenu_Attached_0" jax="CHTML" tabindex="0" ctxtmenu_counter="34" style="font-size: 119%; position: relative;"><mjx-math class="MJX-TEX" aria-hidden="true"><mjx-msub><mjx-texatom texclass="ORD"><mjx-mover><mjx-over style="padding-bottom: 0.105em; <ul>
  <li>데이터 집합 <mjx-container class="MathJax CtxtMenu_Attached_0" jax="CHTML" tabindex="0" ctxtmenu_counter="36" style="font-size: 119%; position: relative;"><mjx-math class="MJX-TEX" aria-hidden="true"><mjx-texatom texclass="ORD"><mjx-mi class="mjx-b"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D417 TEX-B"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-texatom></mjx-math><mjx-assistive-mml unselectable="on" display="inline"><mjx-container class="MathJax CtxtMenu_Attached_0" jax="CHTML" tabindex="0" ctxtmenu_counter="36" style="font-size: 118.6%; position: relative;"><mjx-math class="MJX-TEX" aria-hidden="true"><mjx-texatom texclass="ORD"><mjx-mi class="mjx-b"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D417 TEX-B"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-texatom></mjx-math><mjx-assistive-mml unselectable="on" display="inline"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mrow data-mjx-texclass="ORD"><mi mathvariant="bold">X</mi></mrow></math></mjx-assistive-mml></mjx-container></mjx-assistive-mml></mjx-container>가 독립적으로 추출되었을 경우 로그가능도를 최적화합니다

<ol>
  <li>우도 함수 <mjx-container class="MathJax CtxtMenu_Attached_0" jax="CHTML" tabindex="0" ctxtmenu_counter="38" style="font-size: 119%; position: relative;"><mjx-math class="MJX-TEX" aria-hidden="true"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D43F TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c28"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D703 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c3B"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-texatom space="2" texclass="ORD"><mjx-mi class="mjx-b"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D417 TEX-B"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-texatom><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c29"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-math><mjx-assistive-mml unselectable="on" display="inline"><mjx-container class="MathJax CtxtMenu_Attached_0" jax="CHTML" tabindex="0" ctxtmenu_counter="38" style="font-size: 118.6%; position: relative;"><mjx-math class="MJX-TEX" aria-hidden="true"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D43F TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c28"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D703 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c3B"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-texatom space="2" texclass="ORD"><mjx-mi class="mjx-b"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D417 TEX-B"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-texatom><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c29"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-math><mjx-assistive-mml unselectable="on" display="inline"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mi>L</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>θ</mi><mo>;</mo><mrow data-mjx-texclass="ORD"><mi mathvariant="bold">X</mi></mrow><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></math></mjx-assistive-mml></mjx-container></mjx-assistive-mml></mjx-container> 이해:
    <ul>
      <li>주어진 데이터 <mjx-container class="MathJax CtxtMenu_Attached_0" jax="CHTML" tabindex="0" ctxtmenu_counter="39" style="font-size: 119%; position: relative;"><mjx-math class="MJX-TEX" aria-hidden="true"><mjx-texatom texclass="ORD"><mjx-mi class="mjx-b"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D417 TEX-B"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-texatom></mjx-math><mjx-assistive-mml unselectable="on" display="inline"><mjx-container class="MathJax CtxtMenu_Attached_0" jax="CHTML" tabindex="0" ctxtmenu_counter="39" style="font-size: 118.6%; position: relative;"><mjx-math class="MJX-TEX" aria-hidden="true"><mjx-texatom texclass="ORD"><mjx-mi class="mjx-b"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D417 TEX-B"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-texatom></mjx-math><mjx-assistive-mml unselectable="on" display="inline"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mrow data-mjx-texclass="ORD"><mi mathvariant="bold">X</mi></mrow></math></mjx-assistive-mml></mjx-container></mjx-assistive-mml></mjx-container>가 주어졌을 때,
각 데이터 <mjx-container class="MathJax CtxtMenu_Attached_0" jax="CHTML" tabindex="0" ctxtmenu_counter="40" style="font-size: 119%; position: relative;"><mjx-math class="MJX-TEX" aria-hidden="true"><mjx-msub><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D465 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-script style="vertical-align: -0.15em;"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i" size="s"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D456 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-script></mjx-msub></mjx-math><mjx-assistive-mml unselectable="on" display="inline"><mjx-container class="MathJax CtxtMenu_Attached_0" jax="CHTML" tabindex="0" ctxtmenu_counter="40" style="font-size: 118.6%;       <li>이 곱셈 형태의 우도 함수는 독립적인 사건들의 결합 확률을 나타냅니다.</li>
    </ul>
  </li>
  <li>로그 우도 함수 <mjx-container class="MathJax CtxtMenu_Attached_0" jax="CHTML" tabindex="0" ctxtmenu_counter="43" style="font-size: 119%; position: relative;"><mjx-math class="MJX-TEX" aria-hidden="true"><mjx-mi class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c6C"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c6F"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c67"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2061"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i" space="2"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D43F TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c28"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D703 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c3B"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-texatom space="2" texclass="ORD"><mjx-mi class="mjx-b"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D417 TEX-B"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-texatom><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c29"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-math><mjx-assistive-mml unselectable="on" display="inline"><mjx-container class="MathJax CtxtMenu_Attached_0" jax="CHTML" tabindex="0" ctxtmenu_counter="43" style="font-size: 118.6%; position: relative;"><mjx-math class="MJX-TEX" aria-hidden="true"><mjx-mi class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c6C"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c6F"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c67"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2061"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i" space="2"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D43F TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c28"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D703 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c3B"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-texatom space="2" texclass="ORD"><mjx-mi class="mjx-b"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D417 TEX-B"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-texatom><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c29"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-math><mjx-assistive-mml unselectable="on" display="inline"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mi>log</mi><mo data-mjx-texclass="NONE">⁡</mo><mi>L</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>θ</mi><mo>;</mo><mrow data-mjx-texclass="ORD"><mi mathvariant="bold">X</mi></mrow><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></math></mjx-assistive-mml></mjx-container></mjx-assistive-mml></mjx-container>로 변환:
    <ul>
      <li>우도 함수를 직접 최대화하는 대신, 로그 우도 함수를 최대화하는 것이 더 수학적으로 간편하고 안정적입니다.</li>
      <li>로그 변환을 통해 곱셈을 덧셈으로 변환하면 계산의 복잡성이 줄어듭니다.</li>
    </ul>
  </li>
  <li>최대화 과정:
    <ul>
      <li>로그 우도 함수를 최대화하는 파라미터 <mjx-container class="MathJax CtxtMenu_Attached_0" jax="CHTML" tabindex="0" ctxtmenu_counter="44" style="font-size: 119%; position: relative;"><mjx-math class="MJX-TEX" aria-hidden="true"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D703 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-math><mjx-assistive-mml unselectable="on" display="inline"><mjx-container class="MathJax CtxtMenu_Attached_0" jax="CHTML" tabindex="0" ctxtmenu_counter="44" style="font-size: 118.6%; position: relative;"><mjx-math class="MJX-TEX" aria-hidden="true"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D703 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-math><mjx-assistive-mml unselectable="on" display="inline"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mi>θ</mi></math></mjx-assistive-mml></mjx-container></mjx-assistive-mml></mjx-container>를 찾는 과정은 원래의 우도 함수를 최대화하는 것과 동일한 결과를 줍니다.</li>
      <li>로그 우도 함수의 최대화를 통해 더 효율적이고 안정적으로 최대우도추정치를 구할 수 있습니다.</li>
    </ul>
  </li>
  <li>경사하강법으로 가능도를 최적화할 때 미분 연산을 사용하게 되는데, 로그가능도를 사용하면 연산량을 <mjx-container class="MathJax CtxtMenu_Attached_0" jax="CHTML" tabindex="0" ctxtmenu_counter="45" style="font-size: 119%; position: relative;"><mjx-math class="MJX-TEX" aria-hidden="true"><mjx-texatom texclass="ORD"><mjx-mi class="mjx-cal mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c4F TEX-C"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-texatom><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c28"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-msup><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D45B TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-script style="vertical-align: 0.363em;"><mjx-mn class="mjx-n" size="s"><mjx-c class="mjx-c32"></mjx-c></mjx-mn></mjx-script></mjx-msup><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c29"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-math><mjx-assistive-mml unselectable="on" display="inline"><mjx-container class="MathJax CtxtMenu_Attached_0" jax="CHTML" tabindex="0" ctxtmenu_counter="45" style="font-size: 118.6%; position: relative;"><mjx-math class="MJX-TEX" aria-hidden="true"><mjx-texatom texclass="ORD"><mjx-mi class="mjx-cal mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c4F TEX-C"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-texatom><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c28"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-msup><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D45B TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-script style="vertical-align: 0.363em;"><mjx-mn class="mjx-n" size="s"><mjx-c class="mjx-c32"></mjx-c></mjx-mn></mjx-script></mjx-msup><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c29"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-math><mjx-assistive-mml unselectable="on" display="inline"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mrow data-mjx-texclass="ORD"><mi data-mjx-variant="-tex-calligraphic" mathvariant="script">O</mi></mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msup><mi>n</mi><mn>2</mn></msup><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></math></mjx-assistive-mml></mjx-container></mjx-assistive-mml></mjx-container>에서 <mjx-container class="MathJax CtxtMenu_Attached_0" jax="CHTML" tabindex="0" ctxtmenu_counter="46" style="font-size: 119%; position: relative;"><mjx-math class="MJX-TEX" aria-hidden="true"><mjx-texatom texclass="ORD"><mjx-mi class="mjx-cal mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c4F TEX-C"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-texatom><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c28"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D45B TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c29"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-math><mjx-assistive-mml unselectable="on" display="inline"><mjx-container class="MathJax CtxtMenu_Attached_0" jax="CHTML" tabindex="0" ctxtmenu_counter="46" style="font-size: 118.6%; position: relative;"><mjx-math class="MJX-TEX" aria-hidden="true"><mjx-texatom texclass="ORD"><mjx-mi class="mjx-cal mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c4F TEX-C"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-texatom><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c28"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D45B TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c29"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-math><mjx-assistive-mml unselectable="on" display="inline"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mrow data-mjx-texclass="ORD"><mi data-mjx-variant="-tex-calligraphic" mathvariant="script">O</mi></mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></math></mjx-assistive-mml></mjx-container></mjx-assistive-mml></mjx-container>으로 줄여줌</li>
  <li>대게의 손실함수의 경우 경사하강법을 사용하므로 음의 로그가능도(negative log-likelihood)를 최적화하게 됨</li>
</ol>

<h3 id="최대가능도-추정법-예제-정규분포">최대가능도 추정법 예제: 정규분포<a class="header-link" href="#최대가능도-추정법-예제-정규분포" title="Permalink"><span class="sr-only">Permalink</span><i class="fas fa-link"></i></a></h3>

<ul>
  <li>정규분포를 따르는 확률변수 <mjx-container class="MathJax CtxtMenu_Attached_0" jax="CHTML" tabindex="0" ctxtmenu_counter="47" style="font-size: 119%; position: relative;"><mjx-math class="MJX-TEX" aria-hidden="true"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D44B TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-math><mjx-assistive-mml unselectable="on" display="inline"><mjx-container class="MathJax CtxtMenu_Attached_0" jax="CHTML" tabindex="0" ctxtmenu_counter="47" style="font-size: 118.6%; <h3 id="단계별-설명">단계별 설명<a class="header-link" href="#단계별-설명" title="Permalink"><span class="sr-only">Permalink</span><i class="fas fa-link"></i></a></h3>

<ol>
  <li>최대우도추정(MLE) 정의:</li>
</ol>

<ul>
  <li>MLE는 주어진 데이터 <mjx-container class="MathJax CtxtMenu_Attached_0" jax="CHTML" tabindex="0" ctxtmenu_counter="52" style="font-size: 119%; position: relative;"><mjx-math class="MJX-TEX" aria-hidden="true"><mjx-texatom texclass="ORD"><mjx-mi class="mjx-b"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D417 TEX-B"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-texatom></mjx-math><mjx-assistive-mml unselectable="on" display="inline"><mjx-container class="MathJax CtxtMenu_Attached_0" jax="CHTML" tabindex="0" ctxtmenu_counter="52" style="font-size: 118.6%; position: relative;"><mjx-math class="MJX-TEX" aria-hidden="true"><mjx-texatom texclass="ORD"><mjx-mi class="mjx-b"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D417 TEX-B"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-texatom></mjx-math><mjx-assistive-mml unselectable="on" display="inline"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mrow data-mjx-texclass="ORD"><mi mathvariant="bold">X</mi></mrow></math></mjx-assistive-mml></mjx-container></mjx-assistive-mml></mjx-container>에 대해 파라미터 <mjx-container class="MathJax CtxtMenu_Attached_0" jax="CHTML" tabindex="0" ctxtmenu_counter="53" style="font-size: 119%; position: relative;"><mjx-math class="MJX-TEX" aria-hidden="true"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D703 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-math><mjx-assistive-mml unselectable="on" display="inline"><mjx-container class="MathJax CtxtMenu_Attached_0" jax="CHTML" tabindex="0" ctxtmenu_counter="53" style="font-size: 118.6%; position: relative;"><mjx-math class="MJX-TEX" aria-hidden="true"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D703 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-math><mjx-assistive-mml unselectable="on" display="inline"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mi>θ</mi></math></mjx-assistive-mml></mjx-container></mjx-assistive-mml></mjx-container>를 찾는 방법입니다. 여기서 <mjx-container class="MathJax CtxtMenu_Attached_0" jax="CHTML" tabindex="0" ctxtmenu_counter="54" style="font-size: 119%; position: relative;"><mjx-math class="MJX-TEX" aria-hidden="true"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D703 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-math><mjx-assistive-mml unselectable="on" display="inline"><mjx-container class="MathJax CtxtMenu_Attached_0" jax="CHTML" tabindex="0" ctxtmenu_counter="54" style="font-size: 118.6%; position: relative;"><mjx-math class="MJX-TEX" aria-hidden="true"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D703 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-math><mjx-assistive-mml unselectable="on" display="inline"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mi>θ</mi></math></mjx-assistive-mml></mjx-container></mjx-assistive-mml></mjx-container>는 <mjx-container class="MathJax CtxtMenu_Attached_0" jax="CHTML" tabindex="0" ctxtmenu_counter="55" style="font-size: 119%; position: relative;"><mjx-math class="MJX-TEX" aria-hidden="true"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D707 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-math><mjx-assistive-mml unselectable="on" display="inline"><mjx-container class="MathJax CtxtMenu_Attached_0" jax="CHTML" tabindex="0" ctxtmenu_counter="55" style="font-size: 118.6%; position: relative;"><mjx-math class="MJX-TEX" aria-hidden="true"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D707 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-math><mjx-assistive-mml unselectable="on" display="inline"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mi>μ</mi></math></mjx-assistive-mml></mjx-container></mjx-assistive-mml></mjx-container>와 <mjx-container class="MathJax CtxtMenu_Attached_0" jax="CHTML" tabindex="0" ctxtmenu_counter="56" style="font-size: 119%; position: relative;"><mjx-math class="MJX-TEX" aria-hidden="true"><mjx-msup><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D70E TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-script style="vertical-align: 0.363em;"><mjx-mn class="mjx-n" size="s"><mjx-c class="mjx-c32"></mjx-c></mjx-mn></mjx-script></mjx-msup></mjx-math><mjx-assistive-mml unselectable="on" display="inline"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><msup><mi>σ</mi><mn>2</mn></msup></math></mjx-assistive-mml></mjx-container></mjx-assistive-mml></mjx-container>를 포함합니다.</li>
  <li><mjx-container class="MathJax CtxtMenu_Attached_0" jax="CHTML" tabindex="0" ctxtmenu_counter="57" style="font-size: 119%; position: relative;"><mjx-math class="MJX-TEX" aria-hidden="true"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D703 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-math><mjx-assistive-mml unselectable="on" display="inline"><mjx-container class="MathJax CtxtMenu_Attached_0" jax="CHTML" tabindex="0" ctxtmenu_counter="57" style="font-size: 118.6%; position: relative;"><mjx-math class="MJX-TEX" aria-hidden="true"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D703 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-math><mjx-assistive-mml unselectable="on" display="inline"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mi>θ</mi></math></mjx-assistive-mml></mjx-container></mjx-assistive-mml></mjx-container> 값을 최대화하는 것이 목표입니다.</li>
</ul>

<ol>
  <li>로그 우도 함수 <mjx-container class="MathJax CtxtMenu_Attached_0" jax="CHTML" tabindex="0" ctxtmenu_counter="58" style="font-size: 119%; position: relative;"><mjx-math class="MJX-TEX" aria-hidden="true"><mjx-mi class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c6C"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c6F"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c67"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2061"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i" space="2"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D43F TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c28"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D703 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c3B"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-texatom space="2" texclass="ORD"><mjx-mi class="mjx-b"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D417 TEX-B"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-texatom><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c29"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-math><mjx-assistive-mml unselectable="on" display="inline"><mjx-container class="MathJax CtxtMenu_Attached_0" jax="CHTML" tabindex="0" ctxtmenu_counter="58" style="font-size: 118.6%; position: relative;"><mjx-math class="MJX-TEX" aria-hidden="true"><mjx-mi class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c6C"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c6F"></mjx-c><mjx-c class="mjx-c67"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2061"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i" space="2"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D43F TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c28"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D703 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c3B"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-texatom space="2" texclass="ORD"><mjx-mi class="mjx-b"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D417 TEX-B"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-texatom><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c29"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-math><mjx-assistive-mml unselectable="on" display="inline"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mi>log</mi><mo data-mjx-texclass="NONE">⁡</mo><mi>L</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>θ</mi><mo>;</mo><mrow data-mjx-texclass="ORD"><mi mathvariant="bold">X</mi></mrow><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></math></mjx-assistive-mml></mjx-container></mjx-assistive-mml></mjx-container> 계산:</li>
</ol>

<ul>
  <li>로그 우도 함수는 우도 함수의 로그를 취한 것으로, 계산을 간단하게 합니다.</li>
  <li>주어진 데이터 <mjx-container class="MathJax CtxtMenu_Attached_0" jax="CHTML" tabindex="0" ctxtmenu_counter="59" style="font-size: 119%; position: relative;"><mjx-math class="MJX-TEX" aria-hidden="true"><mjx-texatom texclass="ORD"><mjx-mi class="mjx-b"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D417 TEX-B"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-texatom><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="4"><mjx-c class="mjx-c3D"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-texatom space="4" texclass="ORD"><mjx-msub><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D465 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-script style="vertical-align: -0.15em;"><mjx-mn class="mjx-n" size="s"><mjx-c class="mjx-c31"></mjx-c></mjx-mn></mjx-script></mjx-msub><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2C"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-msub space="2"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D465 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-script style="vertical-align: -0.15em;"><mjx-mn class="mjx-n" size="s"><mjx-c class="mjx-c32"></mjx-c></mjx-mn></mjx-script></mjx-msub><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2C"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="2"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2026"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="2"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2C"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-msub space="2"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D465 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-script style="vertical-align: -0.15em;"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i" size="s"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D45B TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-script></mjx-msub></mjx-texatom></mjx-math><mjx-assistive-mml unselectable="on" display="inline"><mjx-container class="MathJax CtxtMenu_Attached_0" jax="CHTML" tabindex="0" ctxtmenu_counter="59" style="font-size: 118.6%; position: relative;"><mjx-math class="MJX-TEX" aria-hidden="true"><mjx-texatom texclass="ORD"><mjx-mi class="mjx-b"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D417 TEX-B"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-texatom><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="4"><mjx-c class="mjx-c3D"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-texatom space="4" texclass="ORD"><mjx-msub><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D465 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-script style="vertical-align: -0.15em;"><mjx-mn class="mjx-n" size="s"><mjx-c class="mjx-c31"></mjx-c></mjx-mn></mjx-script></mjx-msub><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2C"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-msub space="2"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D465 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-script style="vertical-align: -0.15em;"><mjx-mn class="mjx-n" size="s"><mjx-c class="mjx-c32"></mjx-c></mjx-mn></mjx-script></mjx-msub><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2C"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="2"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2026"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mo class="mjx-n" space="2"><mjx-c class="mjx-c2C"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-msub space="2"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D465 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-script style="vertical-align: -0.15em;"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i" size="s"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D45B TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-script></mjx-msub></mjx-texatom></mjx-math><mjx-assistive-mml unselectable="on" display="inline"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mrow data-mjx-texclass="ORD"><mi mathvariant="bold">X</mi></mrow><mo>=</mo><mrow data-mjx-texclass="ORD"><msub><mi>x</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><mo>,</mo><msub><mi>x</mi><mn>2</mn></msub><mo>,</mo><mo>…</mo><mo>,</mo><msub><mi>x</mi><mi>n</mi></msub></mrow></math></mjx-assistive-mml></mjx-container></mjx-assistive-mml></mjx-container>에 대해 로그 우도 함수는 다음과 같이 계산됩니다:</li>
</ul>

  <li>정규분포의 확률밀도함수(PDF):</li>

<ol>
  <li>로그 우도 함수의 전개:</li>
</ol>

<ul>
  <li>로그 우도 함수를 구하기 위해 각 <mjx-container class="MathJax CtxtMenu_Attached_0" jax="CHTML" tabindex="0" ctxtmenu_counter="63" style="font-size: 119%; position: relative;"><mjx-math class="MJX-TEX" aria-hidden="true"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D443 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c28"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-msub><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D465 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-script style="vertical-align: -0.15em;"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i" size="s"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D456 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-script></mjx-msub><mjx-texatom texclass="ORD"><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c7C"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-texatom><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D703 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c29"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-math><mjx-assistive-mml unselectable="on" display="inline"><mjx-container class="MathJax CtxtMenu_Attached_0" jax="CHTML" tabindex="0" ctxtmenu_counter="63" style="font-size: 118.6%; </ul>

<ul>
  <li>로그 성질을 이용해 우도 함수를 전개하면 다음과 같습니다:</li>

<h3 id="1-로그-우도-함수의-mu에-대한-편미분">1. 로그 우도 함수의 <mjx-container class="MathJax CtxtMenu_Attached_0" jax="CHTML" tabindex="0" ctxtmenu_counter="68" style="font-size: 119%; position: relative;"><mjx-math class="MJX-TEX" aria-hidden="true"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D707 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-math><mjx-assistive-mml unselectable="on" display="inline"><mjx-container class="MathJax CtxtMenu_Attached_0" jax="CHTML" tabindex="0" ctxtmenu_counter="68" style="font-size: 117.2%; position: relative;"><mjx-math class="MJX-TEX" aria-hidden="true"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D707 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-math><mjx-assistive-mml unselectable="on" display="inline"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mi>μ</mi></math></mjx-assistive-mml></mjx-container></mjx-assistive-mml></mjx-container>에 대한 편미분<a class="header-link" href="#1-로그-우도-함수의-mu에-대한-편미분" title="Permalink"><span class="sr-only">Permalink</span><i class="fas fa-link"></i></a></h3>

data-mjx-texclass="ORD"><mi>i</mi><mo>=</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow><mrow data-mjx-texclass="ORD"><mi>n</mi></mrow></munderover><mfrac><mrow><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><msub><mi>x</mi><mi>i</mi></msub><mo>−</mo><mi>μ</mi><msup><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mn>2</mn></msup></mrow><mrow><mn>2</mn><msup><mi>σ</mi><mn>2</mn></msup></mrow></mfrac></math></mjx-assistive-mml></mjx-container></mjx-assistive-mml></mjx-container>

<ul>
  <li><mjx-container class="MathJax CtxtMenu_Attached_0" jax="CHTML" tabindex="0" ctxtmenu_counter="71" style="font-size: 119%; position: relative;"><mjx-math class="MJX-TEX" aria-hidden="true"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D707 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-math><mjx-assistive-mml unselectable="on" display="inline"><mjx-container class="MathJax CtxtMenu_Attached_0" jax="CHTML" tabindex="0" ctxtmenu_counter="71" style="font-size: 118.6%; position: relative;"><mjx-math class="MJX-TEX" aria-hidden="true"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D707 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-math><mjx-assistive-mml unselectable="on" display="inline"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mi>μ</mi></math></mjx-assistive-mml></mjx-container></mjx-assistive-mml></mjx-container>에 대한 편미분:</li>
  <li>로그 우도 함수를 <mjx-container class="MathJax CtxtMenu_Attached_0" jax="CHTML" tabindex="0" ctxtmenu_counter="72" style="font-size: 119%; position: relative;"><mjx-math class="MJX-TEX" aria-hidden="true"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D707 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-math><mjx-assistive-mml unselectable="on" display="inline"><mjx-container class="MathJax CtxtMenu_Attached_0" jax="CHTML" tabindex="0" ctxtmenu_counter="72" style="font-size: 118.6%; position: relative;"><mjx-math class="MJX-TEX" aria-hidden="true"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D707 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-math><mjx-assistive-mml unselectable="on" display="inline"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mi>μ</mi></math></mjx-assistive-mml></mjx-container></mjx-assistive-mml></mjx-container>에 대해 미분합니다.</li>
  <li><mjx-container class="MathJax CtxtMenu_Attached_0" jax="CHTML" tabindex="0" ctxtmenu_counter="73" style="font-size: 119%; position: relative;"><mjx-math class="MJX-TEX" aria-hidden="true"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D707 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-math><mjx-assistive-mml unselectable="on" display="inline"><mjx-container class="MathJax CtxtMenu_Attached_0" jax="CHTML" tabindex="0" ctxtmenu_counter="73" style="font-size: 118.6%; position: relative;"><mjx-math class="MJX-TEX" aria-hidden="true"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D707 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-math><mjx-assistive-mml unselectable="on" display="inline"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mi>μ</mi></math></mjx-assistive-mml></mjx-container></mjx-assistive-mml></mjx-container>에 대한 편미분은 다음과 같이 계산됩니다:</li>

<ul>
  <li>최적화 조건:</li>
  <li>이 편미분 결과를 0으로 설정하여 최적 조건을 찾습니다.</li>
</ul>

display="block"><mn>0</mn><mo>=</mo><mfrac><mrow><mi>∂</mi><mi>log</mi><mo data-mjx-texclass="NONE">⁡</mo><mi>L</mi></mrow><mrow><mi>∂</mi><mi>σ</mi></mrow></mfrac><mo>=</mo><mo>−</mo><mfrac><mi>n</mi><mi>σ</mi></mfrac><mo>+</mo><mfrac><mn>1</mn><msup><mi>σ</mi><mn>3</mn></msup></mfrac><munderover><mo <ul>
  <li>로그 우도 함수:</li>
  <li>동일한 로그 우도 함수에서 <mjx-container class="MathJax CtxtMenu_Attached_0" jax="CHTML" tabindex="0" ctxtmenu_counter="79" style="font-size: 119%; position: relative;"><mjx-math class="MJX-TEX" aria-hidden="true"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D70E TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-math><mjx-assistive-mml unselectable="on" display="inline"><mjx-container class="MathJax CtxtMenu_Attached_0" jax="CHTML" tabindex="0" ctxtmenu_counter="79" style="font-size: 118.6%; position: relative;"><mjx-math class="MJX-TEX" aria-hidden="true"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D70E TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-math><mjx-assistive-mml unselectable="on" display="inline"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mi>σ</mi></math></mjx-assistive-mml></mjx-container></mjx-assistive-mml></mjx-container>에 대해 미분합니다.</li>
  <li><mjx-container class="MathJax CtxtMenu_Attached_0" jax="CHTML" tabindex="0" ctxtmenu_counter="80" style="font-size: 119%; position: relative;"><mjx-math class="MJX-TEX" aria-hidden="true"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D70E TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-math><mjx-assistive-mml unselectable="on" display="inline"><mjx-container class="MathJax CtxtMenu_Attached_0" jax="CHTML" tabindex="0" ctxtmenu_counter="80" style="font-size: 118.6%; position: relative;"><mjx-math class="MJX-TEX" aria-hidden="true"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D70E TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-math><mjx-assistive-mml unselectable="on" display="inline"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mi>σ</mi></math></mjx-assistive-mml></mjx-container></mjx-assistive-mml></mjx-container>에 대한 편미분:</li>
  <li>로그 우도 함수를 <mjx-container class="MathJax CtxtMenu_Attached_0" jax="CHTML" tabindex="0" ctxtmenu_counter="81" style="font-size: 119%; position: relative;"><mjx-math class="MJX-TEX" aria-hidden="true"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D70E TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-math><mjx-assistive-mml unselectable="on" display="inline"><mjx-container class="MathJax CtxtMenu_Attached_0" jax="CHTML" tabindex="0" ctxtmenu_counter="81" style="font-size: 118.6%; position: relative;"><mjx-math class="MJX-TEX" aria-hidden="true"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D70E TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-math><mjx-assistive-mml unselectable="on" display="inline"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mi>σ</mi></math></mjx-assistive-mml></mjx-container></mjx-assistive-mml></mjx-container>에 대해 미분합니다.</li>
  <li><mjx-container class="MathJax CtxtMenu_Attached_0" jax="CHTML" tabindex="0" ctxtmenu_counter="82" style="font-size: 119%; position: relative;"><mjx-math class="MJX-TEX" aria-hidden="true"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D70E TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-math><mjx-assistive-mml unselectable="on" display="inline"><mjx-container class="MathJax CtxtMenu_Attached_0" jax="CHTML" tabindex="0" ctxtmenu_counter="82" style="font-size: 118.6%; position: relative;"><mjx-math class="MJX-TEX" aria-hidden="true"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D70E TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi></mjx-math><mjx-assistive-mml unselectable="on" display="inline"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mi>σ</mi></math></mjx-assistive-mml></mjx-container></mjx-assistive-mml></mjx-container>에 대한 편미분은 다음과 같이 계산됩니다:</li>
</ul>

  <li>이를 계산하면:</li>

<ul>
  <li>최적화 조건:</li>
  <li>이 편미분 결과를 0으로 설정하여 최적 조건을 찾습니다.</li>

class="mjx-c32"></mjx-c></mjx-mn></mjx-script></mjx-msup></mjx-math><mjx-assistive-mml unselectable="on" display="block"><mjx-container class="MathJax CtxtMenu_Attached_0" jax="CHTML" display="true" tabindex="0" ctxtmenu_counter="87" style="font-size: 118.6%; position: relative;"><mjx-math display="true" class="MJX-TEX" aria-hidden="true" style="margin-left: 0px; margin-right: 0px;"><mjx-mn stretchy="false">⟹</mo><mstyle scriptlevel="0"><mspace width="0.278em"></mspace></mstyle><msubsup><mrow data-mjx-texclass="ORD"><mover><mi>σ</mi><mo stretchy="false">^</mo></mover></mrow><mrow stretchy="false">)</mo><mn>2</mn></msup></math></mjx-assistive-mml></mjx-container></mjx-assistive-mml></mjx-container>

<h2 id="확률분포의-거리">확률분포의 거리<a class="header-link" href="#확률분포의-거리" title="Permalink"><span class="sr-only">Permalink</span><i class="fas fa-link"></i></a></h2>

<ul>
  <li>기계학습에서 사용되는 손실함수들은 모델이 학습하는 확률분포와 데이터에서 관찰되는 확률분포의 거리를 통해 유도</li>
  <li>데이터 공간에 두 개의 확률분포 <mjx-container class="MathJax CtxtMenu_Attached_0" jax="CHTML" tabindex="0" ctxtmenu_counter="88" style="font-size: 119%; position: relative;"><mjx-math class="MJX-TEX" aria-hidden="true"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D443 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c28"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D465 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c29"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-math><mjx-assistive-mml unselectable="on" display="inline"><mjx-container class="MathJax CtxtMenu_Attached_0" jax="CHTML" tabindex="0" ctxtmenu_counter="88" style="font-size: 118.6%; position: relative;"><mjx-math class="MJX-TEX" aria-hidden="true"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D443 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c28"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D465 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c29"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-math><mjx-assistive-mml unselectable="on" display="inline"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mi>P</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>x</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></math></mjx-assistive-mml></mjx-container></mjx-assistive-mml></mjx-container>, <mjx-container class="MathJax CtxtMenu_Attached_0" jax="CHTML" tabindex="0" ctxtmenu_counter="89" style="font-size: 119%; position: relative;"><mjx-math class="MJX-TEX" aria-hidden="true"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D444 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c28"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D465 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c29"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-math><mjx-assistive-mml unselectable="on" display="inline"><mjx-container class="MathJax CtxtMenu_Attached_0" jax="CHTML" tabindex="0" ctxtmenu_counter="89" style="font-size: 118.6%; position: relative;"><mjx-math class="MJX-TEX" aria-hidden="true"><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D444 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c28"></mjx-c></mjx-mo><mjx-mi class="mjx-i"><mjx-c class="mjx-c1D465 TEX-I"></mjx-c></mjx-mi><mjx-mo class="mjx-n"><mjx-c class="mjx-c29"></mjx-c></mjx-mo></mjx-math><mjx-assistive-mml unselectable="on" display="inline"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mi>Q</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>x</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></math></mjx-assistive-mml></mjx-container></mjx-assistive-mml></mjx-container>가 있을 경우 두 확률분포 사이의 거리(distance)를 계산할 때 다음과 같은 함수들을 이용
    <ul>
      <li>총변동 거리(Total Variation Distance, TV)</li>
      <li>쿨백-라이블러 발산(Kullback-Leibler Divergence, KL)</li>
      <li>바슈타인 거리(Wasserstein Distance)</li>
    </ul>
  </li>
</ul>

<hr>

<blockquote>
  <p>확률과 가능도의 차이?</p>
</blockquote>

<ol>
  <li>확률:
    <ul>
      <li>상황: 동전을 던지기 전에</li>
      <li>질문: “앞면이 나올 가능성은?”</li>
      <li>답: 0.5 (50%)</li>
    </ul>
  </li>
  <li>가능도:
    <ul>
      <li>상황: 동전을 던진 후 10번 중 7번 앞면이 나왔다면</li>
      <li>질문: “동전이 앞면이 70% 나올 때 이 결과를 잘 설명할 수 있을까?”</li>
      <li>답: 앞면이 70% 나오는 동전이 이 결과를 잘 설명할 수 있습니다.</li>
    </ul>
  </li>
</ol>

<ul>
  <li>요약
    <ul>
      <li>확률은 사건이 일어나기 전에 그 가능성을 생각하는 것.</li>
      <li>가능도는 사건이 일어난 후 그 결과를 보고 조건을 추정하는 것.</li>
    </ul>
  </li>
</ul>

        
      </section>
